Some monsters gain beneficial effects from \"Feed On\" such as Mending or resetting of skills, but this will be indicated in its statistics, usually as a Special ability (see \"Special\" below). Monsters which have \"Feed On Magic\" are capable of destroying magic items such as Battle Magic or Ritual scrolls, magical weapons, enchanted items, etc."},

The caster must hold out one of their hands with the palm out (as a policeman's \"stop\" signal) and must maintain this gesture if the spell is to remain in effect. While doing this, the caster may move freely but may not engage in combat or use any skill, ability, or spell. If a repelled creature cannot retreat any further and the caster approaches the creature within the ten feet, the spell will fail and is lost. Note that some creatures that possess the ability \"Innate Repel\" may use both hands on two separate targets."},

If this spell is cast on another the caster is responsible for providing the weapon reps or the spell fails, likewise if the claw reps are dropped the spell will end. The target may refuse the weapon reps, which will cause the spell to fail. Magic may be cast while claws are active, however spells cannot be touch-cast through the claws. You may temporarily release a claw rep in order to cast spells via packets. The Claws spell is stackable. If a second set is cast while the first is still active, the duration will not reset but the claws will gain +1 damage and become silver. There are no flashes or any other perceptual indications that a Moonlight Mantle is present in combat. Such mantles count as Body when the recipient is struck by effects that bypass armour. The worms can be consumed up to 1 minute after the target's body dissipates. If the target dissipates to resurrect, the worms will still infest the clothing and belongings they left behind for 1 minute. Should anyone besides the caster touch the worms after the original target enters their Death Count, they too will be infected with Carnivorous Worms. The target should stay there, out of game, for this minute to marshal any possible infections. If the spell was stacked, anyone else who is infected receives the stacked version. If the target receives a Life effect during their Death Count, the worms will be killed."},

const RACIAL_CP = 50, DEFAULT_MAX = 10;
function skill(name, costs, prereqs, opts){
  return {
    name,
    costs, // [M,R,T,N,A,W,Mg,Dr,Ba]
    frag: opts&&opts.frag ? opts.frag : 0,
    maxPurchases: opts&&opts.max ? opts.max : DEFAULT_MAX,
    bodyBonus: opts&&opts.body ? opts.body : 0,
    strBonus: opts&&opts.str ? opts.str : 0,
    occupational: opts&&opts.occ ? true : false,
    prereqPerPurchase: opts&&opts.prereqPerPurchase ? true : false,
    _weaponChoice: opts&&opts._weaponChoice ? opts._weaponChoice : null,
    prereqs: prereqs || [],
    desc: opts&&opts.desc ? opts.desc : 'Description coming soon.',
  };
}

// Helper for frag-only skills — fixed frag cost and CP cost, no per-occupation pricing
function fragSkill(name, frag, cp, prereqs, opts){
  return {
    name,
    costs: null, // no per-occupation pricing — cost is fixed
    cp: cp,
    frag: frag,
    maxPurchases: opts&&opts.max ? opts.max : DEFAULT_MAX,
    bodyBonus: opts&&opts.body ? opts.body : 0,
    strBonus: opts&&opts.str ? opts.str : 0,
    prereqPerPurchase: opts&&opts.prereqPerPurchase ? true : false,
    prereqs: prereqs || [],
    desc: opts&&opts.desc ? opts.desc : 'Description coming soon.',
    _fragOnly: true,
  };
}

];


const ALL_ITEMS = [
  ...MONSTER_ABILITIES.map(function(a){ return Object.assign({},a,{_type:'monster'}); }),
  ...SB_SPELLS.map(function(s){ return Object.assign({},s,{_type:'spell',cat:s.sphere}); }),
  ...SKILLS_VERBATIM,
];

// ── State ──
var rows = [];
var nextId = 1;
var activeDropdown = null;
var focusedIndex = -1;

// ── Filter ──
function filterItems(query) {
  var q = (query || '').toLowerCase().trim();
  if (!q) return ALL_ITEMS;
  return ALL_ITEMS.filter(function(item) {
    return (item.name||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1
        || (item.cat||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1
        || (item.desc||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1;
  });
}

// ── Row management ──
function addRow() {
  var id = nextId++;
  rows.push({ id: id, item: null, count: 1 });
  renderRows();
  setTimeout(function() {
    var el = document.getElementById('search-' + id);
    if (el) { el.focus(); openDropdown(id, ''); }
  }, 50);
}

function removeRow(id) {
  rows = rows.filter(function(r){ return r.id !== id; });
  if (activeDropdown === id) activeDropdown = null;
  renderRows();
  updateSummary();
}

function setRowItem(id, item) {
  var row = rows.find(function(r){ return r.id === id; });
  if (row) { row.item = item; updateSummary(); }
}

function setRowCount(id, val) {
  var row = rows.find(function(r){ return r.id === id; });
  if (row) { row.count = Math.max(1, parseInt(val) || 1); updateSummary(); }
}

function renderRows() {
  var container = document.getElementById('rows-container');
  container.innerHTML = '';
  rows.forEach(function(row) {
    var div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'ability-row';
    div.id = 'row-' + row.id;

    var searchWrap = document.createElement('div');
    searchWrap.className = 'search-wrap';

    var searchInput = document.createElement('input');
    searchInput.type = 'text';
    searchInput.className = 'search-input';
    searchInput.id = 'search-' + row.id;
    searchInput.autocomplete = 'off';
    searchInput.spellcheck = false;
    searchInput.placeholder = 'Search skills, spells, or monster abilities\u2026';
    if (row.item) searchInput.value = row.item.name;

    var dropdown = document.createElement('div');
    dropdown.className = 'dropdown-list';
    dropdown.id = 'dropdown-' + row.id;

    (function(rowId) {
      searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
        openDropdown(rowId, searchInput.value);
        if (!searchInput.value && rows.find(function(r){return r.id===rowId;}).item) {
          rows.find(function(r){return r.id===rowId;}).item = null;
          updateSummary();
        }
      });
      searchInput.addEventListener('focus', function() { openDropdown(rowId, searchInput.value); });
      searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') { e.preventDefault(); moveFocus(1); }
        else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') { e.preventDefault(); moveFocus(-1); }
        else if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); selectFocused(rowId); }
        else if (e.key === 'Escape') { closeDropdown(); searchInput.blur(); }
      });
    })(row.id);

    searchWrap.appendChild(searchInput);
    searchWrap.appendChild(dropdown);

    var countInput = document.createElement('input');
    countInput.type = 'number';
    countInput.className = 'count-input';
    countInput.min = '1';
    countInput.value = row.count;
    (function(rowId) {
      countInput.addEventListener('change', function() { setRowCount(rowId, countInput.value); });
      countInput.addEventListener('input', function() { setRowCount(rowId, countInput.value); });
    })(row.id);

    var removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
    removeBtn.className = 'remove-btn';
    removeBtn.innerHTML = '\u2715';
    removeBtn.title = 'Remove';
    (function(rowId) {
      removeBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { removeRow(rowId); });
    })(row.id);

    div.appendChild(searchWrap);
    div.appendChild(countInput);
    div.appendChild(removeBtn);
    container.appendChild(div);
  });
}

// ── Dropdown ──
function openDropdown(id, query) {
  if (activeDropdown && activeDropdown !== id) closeDropdownById(activeDropdown);
  activeDropdown = id;
  focusedIndex = -1;
  var dd = document.getElementById('dropdown-' + id);
  if (!dd) return;
  var filtered = filterItems(query);
  if (!filtered.length) {
    dd.innerHTML = '<div class="dropdown-none">No results found.</div>';
    dd.classList.add('open');
    dd._filtered = [];
    return;
  }
  var monsters = filtered.filter(function(i){ return i._type==='monster'; });
  var spells   = filtered.filter(function(i){ return i._type==='spell'; });
  var skills   = filtered.filter(function(i){ return i._type==='skill'; });
  var html = '';
  var idx = 0;
  function addGroup(label, items, badge, badgeLabel) {
    if (!items.length) return;
    html += '<div class="dropdown-group-label">' + label + '</div>';
    items.forEach(function(item) {
      var level = item.level ? ' \u00b7 Circle ' + item.level : '';
      var cat   = item.cat   ? ' \u00b7 ' + item.cat : '';
      html += '<div class="dropdown-item" data-idx="' + idx + '" '
        + 'onmousedown="selectItem(' + id + ',' + idx + ')" '
        + 'onmouseover="previewItem(' + idx + ')">'
        + '<span class="item-name">' + item.name + cat + level + '</span>'
        + '<span class="item-badge ' + badge + '">' + badgeLabel + '</span>'
        + '</div>';
      idx++;
    });
  }
  addGroup('Monster Abilities', monsters, 'badge-monster', 'Monster');
  addGroup('Spells',            spells,   'badge-spell',   'Spell');
  addGroup('Skills',            skills,   'badge-skill',   'Skill');
  dd.innerHTML = html;
  dd._filtered = filtered;
  dd.classList.add('open');
}

function closeDropdown() {
  if (activeDropdown) { closeDropdownById(activeDropdown); activeDropdown = null; }
  focusedIndex = -1;
}

function closeDropdownById(id) {
  var d = document.getElementById('dropdown-' + id);
  if (d) d.classList.remove('open');
}

function moveFocus(dir) {
  if (!activeDropdown) return;
  var dd = document.getElementById('dropdown-' + activeDropdown);
  if (!dd) return;
  var items = dd.querySelectorAll('.dropdown-item');
  if (!items.length) return;
  if (items[focusedIndex]) items[focusedIndex].classList.remove('focused');
  focusedIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(items.length - 1, focusedIndex + dir));
  if (items[focusedIndex]) {
    items[focusedIndex].classList.add('focused');
    items[focusedIndex].scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest' });
  }
  if (dd._filtered && dd._filtered[focusedIndex]) showDetail(dd._filtered[focusedIndex]);
}

function selectFocused(id) {
  if (focusedIndex < 0) return;
  var dd = document.getElementById('dropdown-' + id);
  if (!dd || !dd._filtered) return;
  var item = dd._filtered[focusedIndex];
  if (item) applySelection(id, item);
}

function selectItem(id, idx) {
  var dd = document.getElementById('dropdown-' + id);
  if (!dd || !dd._filtered) return;
  var item = dd._filtered[idx];
  if (item) applySelection(id, item);
}

function applySelection(id, item) {
  setRowItem(id, item);
  var input = document.getElementById('search-' + id);
  if (input) input.value = item.name;
  closeDropdown();
  showDetail(item);
  updateSummary();
}

function previewItem(idx) {
  if (!activeDropdown) return;
  var dd = document.getElementById('dropdown-' + activeDropdown);
  if (!dd || !dd._filtered) return;
  var item = dd._filtered[idx];
  if (item) showDetail(item);
}

// ── Detail panel ──
function showDetail(item) {
  var panel = document.getElementById('detail-panel');
  if (!item) { panel.innerHTML = '<div class="detail-empty">Hover a dropdown item to see details</div>'; return; }
  var tc = item._type === 'spell' ? 'spell' : item._type === 'monster' ? 'monster' : 'skill';
  var tl = item._type === 'spell' ? 'Spell' : item._type === 'monster' ? 'Monster Ability' : 'Skill';
  var catTag = item.cat   ? '<span class="detail-tag">' + item.cat + '</span>' : '';
  var lvlTag = item.level ? '<span class="detail-tag">Circle ' + item.level + '</span>' : '';
  var callHtml = (item.call && item.call.indexOf('(Passive') !== 0)
    ? '<div class="detail-incant">Call: ' + item.call + '</div>' : '';
  var incHtml = item.incant
    ? '<div class="detail-incant">Incant: ' + item.incant + '</div>' : '';
  panel.innerHTML = '<div class="detail-name">' + item.name + '</div>'
    + '<div class="detail-meta-row"><span class="detail-tag ' + tc + '">' + tl + '</span>' + catTag + lvlTag + '</div>'
    + callHtml + incHtml
    + '<div class="detail-desc">' + (item.desc || '') + '</div>';
}

// ── Summary ──
function updateSummary() {
  var typeVal   = document.getElementById('inp-type').value.trim();
  var bodyVal   = document.getElementById('inp-body').value.trim();
  var apVal     = document.getElementById('inp-ap').value.trim();
  var damageVal = document.getElementById('inp-damage').value.trim();

  var sumType = document.getElementById('sum-type');
  sumType.textContent = typeVal || '\u2014';
  sumType.style.color      = typeVal ? '' : 'var(--color-text-tertiary)';
  sumType.style.fontStyle  = typeVal ? 'normal' : 'italic';
  sumType.style.fontWeight = typeVal ? '500' : '400';
  sumType.style.fontSize   = typeVal ? '16px' : '13px';
  document.getElementById('sum-body').textContent   = bodyVal   || '\u2014';
  document.getElementById('sum-ap').textContent     = apVal     || '\u2014';
  document.getElementById('sum-damage').textContent = damageVal || '\u2014';

  var tagsEl = document.getElementById('summary-tags');
  var filled = rows.filter(function(r){ return r.item; });
  if (!filled.length) {
    tagsEl.innerHTML = '<span class="summary-empty-note">No skills, spells, or abilities added yet.</span>';
    return;
  }
  tagsEl.innerHTML = filled.map(function(r) {
    var item = r.item;
    var tc = item._type==='spell' ? 'is-spell' : item._type==='monster' ? 'is-monster' : 'is-skill';
    var cnt = r.count > 1 ? ' <span style="font-weight:bold">\u00d7' + r.count + '</span>' : '';
    var typeLabel = item._type==='spell' ? (item.cat||'') + ' Spell' + (item.level ? ', Circle '+item.level : '')
                  : item._type==='monster' ? 'Monster Ability' : (item.cat || 'Skill');
    var callLine = '';
    if (item.call && item.call.indexOf('(Passive') !== 0) {
      callLine = '<div class="sum-entry-call">Call: ' + item.call + '</div>';
    } else if (item.incant) {
      callLine = '<div class="sum-entry-call">Incant: ' + item.incant + '</div>';
    }
    return '<div class="sum-entry ' + tc + '">'
      + '<div class="sum-entry-header">'
      + '<span class="sum-entry-name">' + item.name + cnt + '</span>'
      + '<span class="sum-entry-type">' + typeLabel + '</span>'
      + '</div>'
      + callLine
      + '<div class="sum-entry-desc">' + (item.desc || '') + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

// ── Print ──
function printMonster() {
  var typeVal  = document.getElementById('inp-type').value.trim()   || 'Unnamed Monster';
  var bodyVal  = document.getElementById('inp-body').value.trim()   || '\u2014';
  var apVal    = document.getElementById('inp-ap').value.trim()     || '\u2014';
  var dmgVal   = document.getElementById('inp-damage').value.trim() || '\u2014';
  var filled   = rows.filter(function(r){ return r.item; });
  var monRows  = filled.filter(function(r){ return r.item._type === 'monster'; });
  var spRows   = filled.filter(function(r){ return r.item._type === 'spell'; });
  var skRows   = filled.filter(function(r){ return r.item._type === 'skill'; });

  function entryHtml(r) {
    var item = r.item;
    var cnt  = r.count > 1 ? ' x' + r.count : '';
    var typeLabel = item._type === 'spell'
      ? (item.cat || '') + ' Spell' + (item.level ? ', Circle ' + item.level : '')
      : item._type === 'monster' ? 'Monster Ability' : (item.cat || 'Skill');
    var callLine = '';
    if (item.call && item.call.indexOf('(Passive') !== 0) {
      callLine = '<p style="margin:3px 0 4px;padding:3px 8px;border-left:2px solid #999;font-size:10px;font-style:italic;color:#333">Call: ' + item.call + '</p>';
    } else if (item.incant) {
      callLine = '<p style="margin:3px 0 4px;padding:3px 8px;border-left:2px solid #999;font-size:10px;font-style:italic;color:#333">Incant: ' + item.incant + '</p>';
    }
    return '<div style="margin-bottom:12px;padding-bottom:12px;border-bottom:1px solid #ddd;page-break-inside:avoid">'
      + '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:baseline">'
      + '<strong style="font-size:13px">' + item.name + cnt + '</strong>'
      + '<span style="font-size:9px;color:#666;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px">' + typeLabel + '</span>'
      + '</div>'
      + callLine
      + '<p style="margin:3px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:#222;line-height:1.55">' + (item.desc || '') + '</p>'
      + '</div>';
  }

  function section(label, items) {
    if (!items.length) return '';
    return '<h3 style="font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;border-bottom:2px solid #111;margin:18px 0 10px;padding-bottom:3px">'
      + label + ' (' + items.length + ')</h3>'
      + items.map(entryHtml).join('');
  }

  document.getElementById('print-area').innerHTML =
    '<div style="font-family:Georgia,serif;padding:20px;color:#111;max-width:740px;margin:0 auto">'
    + '<h1 style="font-size:22px;border-bottom:3px solid #111;margin-bottom:10px;padding-bottom:6px">' + typeVal + '</h1>'
    + '<table style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:14px;border-bottom:1px solid #ccc"><tr>'
    + '<td style="padding:4px 28px 8px 0"><div style="font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;color:#666">Body</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:bold">' + bodyVal + '</div></td>'
    + '<td style="padding:4px 28px 8px 0"><div style="font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;color:#666">Armour Points</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:bold">' + apVal + '</div></td>'
    + '<td style="padding:4px 28px 8px 0"><div style="font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;color:#666">Damage</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:bold">' + dmgVal + '</div></td>'
    + '<td style="padding:4px 28px 8px 0"><div style="font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;color:#666">Total Abilities</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:bold">' + filled.length + '</div></td>'
    + '</tr></table>'
    + section('Monster Abilities', monRows)
    + section('Spells', spRows)
    + section('Skills & Vocational', skRows)
    + '</div>';

  window.print();
}

// ── Close dropdown on outside click ──
document.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
  if (!activeDropdown) return;
  var wrap = document.getElementById('row-' + activeDropdown);
  if (wrap && !wrap.contains(e.target)) {
    var row = rows.find(function(r){ return r.id === activeDropdown; });
    var inp = document.getElementById('search-' + activeDropdown);
    if (row && inp) inp.value = row.item ? row.item.name : '';
    closeDropdown();
  }
});

// ── Init ──
addRow();
updateSummary();
</script>
</body>
</html>
